`AlertContainer.cc`:

```cc
#include <AlertContainer.hh>

void AlertContainer::InsertAlert(const Alert& alert) {
  std::unique_lock lock(mutex_);

  for ( const auto& alert_ptr : observers_ ) {
    alert_ptr->OnAlert(alert);
  }
}

AlertContainer& AlertContainer::GetInstance() {
  static AlertContainer instance;
  return instance;
}



```

`AlertMemoryObserver.cc`:

```cc
#include <AlertMemoryObserver.hh>

void AlertMemoryObserver::OnAlert(const Alert& alert) {
  if (!alerted_processes_.contains(alert.process_id)) {
    std::println("[ALERT] PID: {} {}", alert.process_id, alert.text);
    alerted_processes_.insert(alert.process_id);
  }
}
```

`AnalysisEngine.cc`:

```cc
#include <AnalysisEngine.hh>


AnalysisEngine::~AnalysisEngine() = default;

/**
 * @brief This runs the entire analysis
 * @TODO This will need to be refactored.
 */
void AnalysisEngine::Run() {
  std::unique_lock lock(thread_events_mutex_);
  // for each process
  auto& logger = Logger::GetInstance();
  const auto process_list = store_.GetProcesses();
  logger.Logln(std::format("Running analysis on {} processes", process_list.size()) );
  for (const auto& [pid, process] : process_list) {
    // if we don't have any marked image loads, then who even cares.
    const auto& image_loads =  process.GetImageLoads();
    logger.Logln(std::format("Process Id {} has {} Image loads", pid, image_loads.size()) );

    if ( image_loads.empty() ) continue;
    const auto& threads = process.GetThreads();
    logger.Logln(std::format("Process Id {} has {} threads.", pid, threads.size()) );

    size_t patched_thread_count = 0;

    for (const auto& [tid, thread] : threads ) {
      //Get Previous cycle thread events.
      ThreadEvents current_thread_events{};
      ThreadEvents previous_thread_events{};

      current_thread_events.CLR = thread.GetEventCount(ImageLoad::Clr);
      current_thread_events.WinHTTP = thread.GetEventCount(ImageLoad::WinHTTP);
      current_thread_events.Wininet = thread.GetEventCount(ImageLoad::Wininet);

      thread_events_.insert({tid, current_thread_events});

      if ( auto it = previous_thread_events_.find(tid); it != previous_thread_events_.end() ) {
        previous_thread_events = it->second;
      }

      // if current is less-than or equal previous, we have no new alerts.
      if (previous_thread_events_.contains(tid) && (
        (current_thread_events.CLR <= previous_thread_events.CLR && image_loads.contains(ImageLoad::Clr)) ||
          (current_thread_events.WinHTTP <= previous_thread_events.WinHTTP && image_loads.contains(ImageLoad::WinHTTP)) ||
          (current_thread_events.Wininet <= previous_thread_events.Wininet && image_loads.contains(ImageLoad::Wininet))
        )){
        ++patched_thread_count;
      }
    } // thread

    if ( patched_thread_count == threads.size() ) {
      Alert alert{};
      alert.process_id = pid;
      alert.text = "Potential ETW Patching has been detected.";
      alert.timestamp = std::time(nullptr);
      alert.title = "[ETW ALERT]";
      alert_ptr_.InsertAlert(alert);
    }
  } // process

  // finished now so set previous to current and crack on.
  previous_thread_events_ = thread_events_;
  thread_events_.clear();
} // Run();

/**
 * @brief Callback to handle thread exits.
 * @param thread_id The thread identifier to remove
 */
void AnalysisEngine::OnThreadExit(unsigned int thread_id){
  std::unique_lock lock(thread_events_mutex_);
  if ( previous_thread_events_.contains(thread_id) ) {
    previous_thread_events_.erase(thread_id);
  }
}
```

`App.cc`:

```cc
#include <App.hh>


/**
 * @brief
 */
App::App() {
  // Set Config defaults.
  config_.Set("etw.wininet", false);
  config_.Set("etw.winhttp", false);
  config_.Set("etw.clr", false);
  config_.Set("logging.debug.enabled", false);
  config_.Set("logging.stdout.enabled", false);
  config_.Set("logging.file.enabled", false);
  config_.Set<std::string>("logging.file.path", "etw-detector.log");

  auto& logger = Logger::GetInstance();

  if (logger.RegisterObserver(std::make_shared<LogDebug>()) == false )
    throw std::logic_error("Failed to set LogDebug");

  if (logger.RegisterObserver(std::make_shared<LogStdout>()) == false )
    throw std::logic_error("Failed to set LogStdout");

  if (auto& alert_container = AlertContainer::GetInstance();
      alert_container.RegisterObserver(std::make_shared<AlertMemoryObserver>()) == false)
    throw std::logic_error("Failed to set AlertMemoryObserver");

}

/**
 * @brief Runs the main app
 */
void App::Run() {
  std::thread etwThread(&App::RunEtwConsumer, this);
  std::thread IpcThread(&App::RunNamedPipe, this);
  std::thread AnalysisThread(&App::RunAnalysisThread, this);

  IpcThread.join();
  etwThread.join();
  AnalysisThread.join();
}
void App::Stop() {
  is_running_ = false;
}
App& App::LoadFromConfig() {

  return *this;
}
App& App::EnableWininetEtw() {
  config_.Reset("etw.wininet", true);
  return *this;
}
App& App::EnableWinhttpEtw() {
  config_.Reset("etw.winhttp", true);
  return *this;
}
App& App::EnableClrEtw() {
  config_.Reset("etw.clr", true);
  return *this;
}
App& App::EnableDebugLogging() {
  config_.Reset("logging.debug.enabled", true);
  return *this;
}
App& App::EnableFileLogging() {
  config_.Reset("logging.file.enabled", true);
  return *this;
}
App& App::SetFileLoggingPath(std::string path) {
  config_.Reset("logging.file.path", path);
  return *this;
}

/**
 * @brief starts the named pipe IPC thread
 */
void App::RunNamedPipe() {
  try {
    Ipc IPC(L"\\\\.\\pipe\\Etw");
    IPC.Listen();
  }catch (const std::exception& e) {
    Logger::GetInstance().Logln(e.what());
  }
}

/**
 * @brief Starts the ETW consumer thread
 * @TODO Refactor
 */
void App::RunEtwConsumer() {
  try {
    std::wstring etw_name = L"EtwConsumer";
    krabs::user_trace trace(etw_name);

    krabs::provider<> wininet_provider(L"Microsoft-Windows-WinINet");
    krabs::provider<> winhttp_provider(L"Microsoft-Windows-WinHttp");
    krabs::provider<> dotnet_provider(L"Microsoft-Windows-DotNETRuntime");

    std::unordered_map<GUID, ImageLoad> providers = {
      {{0x43d1a55c, 0x76d6, 0x4f7e, {0x99, 0x5c, 0x64, 0xc7, 0x11, 0xe5, 0xca, 0xfe}}, ImageLoad::Wininet}, // WinINet
      {{0x7D44233D, 0x3055, 0x4B9C, {0xBA, 0x64, 0x0D, 0x47, 0xCA, 0x40, 0xA2, 0x32}}, ImageLoad::WinHTTP}, // WinHttp
      {{0xE13C0D23, 0xCCBC, 0x4E12, {0x93, 0x1B, 0xD9, 0xCC, 0x2E, 0xEE, 0x27, 0xE4}}, ImageLoad::Clr} // .NET Runtime
    };
    auto& logger = Logger::GetInstance();
    auto etw_callback = [&providers, &logger](const EVENT_RECORD &rec, const krabs::trace_context &trace_context) {
      auto& store = Storage::GetInstance();

      const auto provider_guid = rec.EventHeader.ProviderId;

      const auto pid = rec.EventHeader.ProcessId;
      const auto tid = rec.EventHeader.ThreadId;

     if (const auto it = providers.find(provider_guid); it != providers.end()) {
        store.IncrementThreadEventCount(it->second, pid, tid);
      }
    };
    dotnet_provider.any(0xf0010000000003ff);
    dotnet_provider.add_on_event_callback(etw_callback);

    winhttp_provider.any(0xf0010000000003ff);
    winhttp_provider.add_on_event_callback(etw_callback);

    wininet_provider.any(0xf0010000000003ff);
    wininet_provider.add_on_event_callback(etw_callback);

    trace.enable(dotnet_provider);
    trace.enable(winhttp_provider);
    trace.enable(wininet_provider);
    logger.Logln("[ ETW ] Starting ETW consumer.");
    trace.start();

    trace.stop();
  }catch (std::exception& e) {
    Logger::GetInstance().Logln(e.what());
  }
}

/**
 * @brief runs the analysis
 */
void App::RunAnalysisThread() {
  try {
    auto& store = Storage::GetInstance();
    auto& alerter = AlertContainer::GetInstance();
    AnalysisEngine analysis(store, alerter);
    while (is_running_) {
      Sleep(60000);
      analysis.Run();
    }
  } catch (std::exception& e) {
    Logger::GetInstance().Logln(e.what());
  }
}
/**
 * @brief
 */
void App::RunTUIThread() {}
```

```txt
    add_subdirectory(Test)
```

`EtwDriver/EtwDriver/Comms.cpp`:

```cpp
#include "Comms.h"
#include "Comms.tmh"



volatile LONG g_ReconnectInProgress = 0;

NTSTATUS SendMessage(const Message& msg) {

    ExAcquireFastMutex(&g_PipeLock);
    HANDLE pipe = g_NamedPipeHandler;
    ExReleaseFastMutex(&g_PipeLock);

    if (pipe == nullptr) {
        if (InterlockedCompareExchange(&g_ReconnectInProgress, 1, 0) != 0) {
            TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER,
                "SendMessage::STATUS_DEVICE_NOT_CONNECTED failed");
            return STATUS_DEVICE_NOT_CONNECTED;
        }

        HANDLE newPipe = nullptr;
        NTSTATUS status = ConnectNamedPipe(&newPipe, ETW_PIPE_NAME);

        ExAcquireFastMutex(&g_PipeLock);
        if (NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
            g_NamedPipeHandler = newPipe;
            pipe = newPipe;
        }
        ExReleaseFastMutex(&g_PipeLock);

        InterlockedExchange(&g_ReconnectInProgress, 0);

        if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
            TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER,
                "ConnectNamedPipe failed %!STATUS!", status);
            return status;
        }
    }

    IO_STATUS_BLOCK ioStatus{};
    Message localMsg = msg;
    NTSTATUS status = ZwWriteFile(pipe, NULL, NULL, NULL,
        &ioStatus, &localMsg, sizeof(Message),
        NULL, NULL);
    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        ExAcquireFastMutex(&g_PipeLock);
        if (g_NamedPipeHandler == pipe) {
            ZwClose(g_NamedPipeHandler);
            g_NamedPipeHandler = nullptr;
        }
        ExReleaseFastMutex(&g_PipeLock);
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER,
            "ZwWriteFile failed %!STATUS!", status);
    }
    return status;
}


NTSTATUS ConnectNamedPipe(PHANDLE hPipe, const wchar_t* etwPipeName) {
    IO_STATUS_BLOCK ioStatus = { 0 };
    UNICODE_STRING pipeName;
    OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES objAttr;

    RtlInitUnicodeString(&pipeName, etwPipeName);
    InitializeObjectAttributes(&objAttr, &pipeName, OBJ_KERNEL_HANDLE | OBJ_CASE_INSENSITIVE, NULL, NULL);

    NTSTATUS status = ZwCreateFile(
        hPipe,
        GENERIC_WRITE,
        &objAttr,
        &ioStatus,
        NULL,
        FILE_ATTRIBUTE_NORMAL,
        FILE_SHARE_READ | FILE_SHARE_WRITE,
        FILE_OPEN,
        FILE_SYNCHRONOUS_IO_NONALERT | FILE_NON_DIRECTORY_FILE,
        NULL,
        0
    );

    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "ZwCreateFile failed %!STATUS!", status);
    }

    return status;
}
```

`EtwDriver/EtwDriver/Comms.h`:

```h
#pragma once
#include <ntddk.h>
#include "config.h"
#include "trace.h"


extern HANDLE g_NamedPipeHandler;
extern FAST_MUTEX g_PipeLock;

extern volatile LONG g_ReconnectInProgress;

enum class ImageLoad {
    Clr = 0,
    Wininet,
    WinHTTP
};

struct ProcessCreation {
    LARGE_INTEGER creation_time;
    unsigned long process_id;
};

struct ProcessExit {
    unsigned long process_id;
};

struct ThreadCreation {
    LARGE_INTEGER creation_time;
    unsigned long process_id;
    unsigned long thread_id;
};

struct ThreadExit {
    unsigned long process_id;
    unsigned long thread_id;
};

struct ImageLoadEvt {
    LARGE_INTEGER load_time;
    unsigned long process_id;
    unsigned long thread_id;
    ImageLoad image_load;
};

enum class Tag {
    ProcessCreation = 0,
    ProcessExit = 1,
    ThreadCreation = 2,
    ThreadExit = 3,
    ImageLoad = 4,
};

struct Message {
    Tag tag;
    union {
        ProcessCreation creation;
        ProcessExit exit;
        ThreadCreation thread_creation;
        ThreadExit thread_exit;
        ImageLoadEvt image_load;
    };
};

NTSTATUS SendMessage(const Message& msg);
NTSTATUS ConnectNamedPipe(PHANDLE hPipe, const wchar_t* etwPipeName);

```

`EtwDriver/EtwDriver/Driver.cpp`:

```cpp
#include "driver.h"
#include "driver.tmh"
#include "config.h"
#include "Notifications.h"

HANDLE g_NamedPipeHandler = nullptr;
FAST_MUTEX g_PipeLock;
WDFDEVICE g_WorkerDevice = nullptr;


#ifdef ALLOC_PRAGMA
#pragma alloc_text (INIT, DriverEntry)
#endif

NTSTATUS
DriverEntry(
    _In_ PDRIVER_OBJECT  DriverObject,
    _In_ PUNICODE_STRING RegistryPath
    ){

    NTSTATUS status = STATUS_SUCCESS;
    WDFDRIVER driver;

    WPP_INIT_TRACING(DriverObject, RegistryPath);
    TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! Entry");

    status = InitialiseWdfDriver(DriverObject, RegistryPath, &driver);
    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        WPP_CLEANUP(DriverObject);
        return status;
    }

    status = InitialiseControlDevice(driver);
    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        WPP_CLEANUP(DriverObject);
        return status;
    }

    InitialiseComms();

    status = RegisterNotificationCallbacks();
    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        WPP_CLEANUP(DriverObject);
        return status;
    }

    return STATUS_SUCCESS;


}

VOID EtwDriverEvtDriverUnload(_In_ WDFDRIVER Driver){
    TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! Entry");

    NTSTATUS status = STATUS_SUCCESS;

    status = PsSetCreateProcessNotifyRoutine(PcreateProcessNotifyRoutine, true);

    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "PsSetCreateProcessNotifyRoutine (removal) failed %!STATUS!", status);
    }

    status = PsRemoveCreateThreadNotifyRoutine(PcreateThreadNotifyRoutine);

    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "PsRemoveCreateThreadNotifyRoutine failed %!STATUS!", status);
    }

    status = PsRemoveLoadImageNotifyRoutine(PloadImageNotifyRoutine);

    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "PsRemoveLoadImageNotifyRoutine failed %!STATUS!", status);
    }

    if (g_NamedPipeHandler != nullptr) {
        status = ZwClose(g_NamedPipeHandler);

        if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
            TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "ZwClose (removal) failed %!STATUS!", status);
        }
        else {
            g_NamedPipeHandler = nullptr;
        }
    }
    WPP_CLEANUP(WdfDriverWdmGetDriverObject(Driver));
}


NTSTATUS InitialiseWdfDriver(PDRIVER_OBJECT DriverObject, PUNICODE_STRING RegistryPath, WDFDRIVER* OutDriver)
{
    WDF_DRIVER_CONFIG config;
    NTSTATUS status = STATUS_SUCCESS;
    WDF_OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES driverAttributes;


    WDF_OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES_INIT(&driverAttributes);
    WDF_DRIVER_CONFIG_INIT(&config, WDF_NO_EVENT_CALLBACK);
    config.DriverInitFlags |= WdfDriverInitNonPnpDriver;
    config.EvtDriverUnload = EtwDriverEvtDriverUnload;


    status = WdfDriverCreate(DriverObject,
        RegistryPath,
        &driverAttributes,
        &config,
        OutDriver
    );

    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "WdfDriverCreate failed %!STATUS!", status);
        return status;
    }


    return status;
}
NTSTATUS InitialiseControlDevice(WDFDRIVER Driver)
{
    WDF_OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES deviceAttributes;
    PWDFDEVICE_INIT DeviceInit = nullptr;
    NTSTATUS status = STATUS_SUCCESS;

    DeviceInit = WdfControlDeviceInitAllocate(Driver, &SDDL_DEVOBJ_SYS_ALL_ADM_ALL);

    if (DeviceInit == nullptr) {
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "WdfControlDeviceInitAllocate failed with nullptr.");
        return STATUS_INSUFFICIENT_RESOURCES;
    }

    WdfDeviceInitSetDeviceType(DeviceInit, FILE_DEVICE_UNKNOWN);
    WdfDeviceInitSetCharacteristics(DeviceInit, FILE_DEVICE_SECURE_OPEN, TRUE);

    WDF_OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES_INIT(&deviceAttributes);
    TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "About to call WdfDeviceCreate, DeviceInit: %p", DeviceInit);

    status = WdfDeviceCreate(&DeviceInit, &deviceAttributes, &g_WorkerDevice);

    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        WdfDeviceInitFree(DeviceInit);
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "WdfDeviceCreate failed %!STATUS!", status);
        return status;
    }

    WdfControlFinishInitializing(g_WorkerDevice);

    return status;
}
void InitialiseComms(){
    NTSTATUS status = STATUS_SUCCESS;
    // create mutex
    ExInitializeFastMutex(&g_PipeLock);

    status = ConnectNamedPipe(&g_NamedPipeHandler, ETW_PIPE_NAME);

    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "ConnectNamedPipe failed %!STATUS!", status);
    }
}

NTSTATUS RegisterNotificationCallbacks()
{
    NTSTATUS status = STATUS_SUCCESS;
    BOOLEAN processNotifyRegistered = FALSE;
    BOOLEAN threadNotifyRegistered = FALSE;
    BOOLEAN imageNotifyRegistered = FALSE;

    status = PsSetCreateProcessNotifyRoutine(PcreateProcessNotifyRoutine, FALSE);
    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER,
            "PsSetCreateProcessNotifyRoutine failed %!STATUS!", status);
        goto cleanup;
    }
    processNotifyRegistered = TRUE;

    status = PsSetCreateThreadNotifyRoutine(PcreateThreadNotifyRoutine);
    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER,
            "PsSetCreateThreadNotifyRoutine failed %!STATUS!", status);
        goto cleanup;
    }
    threadNotifyRegistered = TRUE;

    status = PsSetLoadImageNotifyRoutine(PloadImageNotifyRoutine);
    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER,
            "PsSetLoadImageNotifyRoutine failed %!STATUS!", status);
        goto cleanup;
    }
    imageNotifyRegistered = TRUE;

    return STATUS_SUCCESS;

cleanup:
    if (imageNotifyRegistered)
        PsRemoveLoadImageNotifyRoutine(PloadImageNotifyRoutine);
    if (threadNotifyRegistered)
        PsRemoveCreateThreadNotifyRoutine(PcreateThreadNotifyRoutine);
    if (processNotifyRegistered)
        PsSetCreateProcessNotifyRoutine(PcreateProcessNotifyRoutine, TRUE);

    return status;
}


void UnregisterNotificationCallbacks() {
    NTSTATUS status;

    status = PsSetCreateProcessNotifyRoutine(PcreateProcessNotifyRoutine, true);
    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status))
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER,
            "PsSetCreateProcessNotifyRoutine (removal) failed %!STATUS!", status);

    status = PsRemoveCreateThreadNotifyRoutine(PcreateThreadNotifyRoutine);
    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status))
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER,
            "PsRemoveCreateThreadNotifyRoutine failed %!STATUS!", status);

    status = PsRemoveLoadImageNotifyRoutine(PloadImageNotifyRoutine);
    if (!NT_SUCCESS(status))
        TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER,
            "PsRemoveLoadImageNotifyRoutine failed %!STATUS!", status);
}
```

`EtwDriver/EtwDriver/Notifications.cpp`:

```cpp
#include "Notifications.h"
#include "worker.h"
#include "Notifications.tmh"

VOID PcreateProcessNotifyRoutine(HANDLE ParentId,	HANDLE ProcessId,BOOLEAN Create){
	UNREFERENCED_PARAMETER(ParentId);
	TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! Entry");

	Message msg{};

	
	if (Create) {
		msg.tag = Tag::ProcessCreation;
		KeQuerySystemTimePrecise(&msg.creation.creation_time);
		msg.creation.process_id = HandleToULong(ProcessId);
	}else {
		msg.tag = Tag::ProcessExit;
		msg.exit.process_id = HandleToULong(ProcessId);
	}

	NTSTATUS status = EnqueueMessage(msg);

	if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! EnqueueMessage failed");
	}
}


VOID PcreateThreadNotifyRoutine(HANDLE ProcessId, HANDLE ThreadId, BOOLEAN Create){
	TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! Entry");
	Message msg{};

	if (Create) {
		KeQuerySystemTimePrecise(&msg.thread_creation.creation_time);
		msg.tag = Tag::ThreadCreation;
		msg.thread_creation.process_id = HandleToULong(ProcessId);
		msg.thread_creation.thread_id = HandleToULong(ThreadId);
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! ThreadStart Event");
	}
	else {
		msg.tag = Tag::ThreadExit;
		msg.thread_exit.process_id = HandleToULong(ProcessId);
		msg.thread_exit.thread_id = HandleToULong(ThreadId);
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! ThreadExit Event");
	}

	NTSTATUS status = EnqueueMessage(msg);

	if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! EnqueueMessage failed");
	}
}


VOID PloadImageNotifyRoutine(
	PUNICODE_STRING FullImageName,
	HANDLE ProcessId,
	PIMAGE_INFO ImageInfo
)
{
	UNREFERENCED_PARAMETER(ImageInfo);
	TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! Entry");

	if (!FullImageName || FullImageName->Length == 0 || FullImageName->Buffer == NULL) {
		return;
	}


	UNICODE_STRING clr;
	UNICODE_STRING winhttp;
	UNICODE_STRING wininet;

	RtlInitUnicodeString(&clr, L"\\clr.dll");
	RtlInitUnicodeString(&wininet, L"\\wininet.dll");
	RtlInitUnicodeString(&winhttp, L"\\winhttp.dll");

	Message msg{};
	msg.tag = Tag::ImageLoad;
	KeQuerySystemTimePrecise(&msg.image_load.load_time);
	msg.image_load.process_id = HandleToULong(ProcessId);
	msg.image_load.thread_id = HandleToULong(PsGetCurrentThreadId());

	if (RtlSuffixUnicodeString(&clr, FullImageName, TRUE)) {
		msg.image_load.image_load = ImageLoad::Clr;
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! CLR Image load Event");
	}else if (RtlSuffixUnicodeString(&winhttp, FullImageName,  TRUE)) {
		msg.image_load.image_load = ImageLoad::WinHTTP;
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! WinHTTP Image load Event");
	}else if (RtlSuffixUnicodeString(&wininet, FullImageName, TRUE)) {
		msg.image_load.image_load = ImageLoad::Wininet;
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! Wininet Image load Event");
	}else {
		return;
	}

	NTSTATUS status = EnqueueMessage(msg); 
	
	if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) { 
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "%!FUNC! EnqueueMessage failed");
	}
}
```

`EtwDriver/EtwDriver/Trace.h`:

```h
/*++

Module Name:

    Trace.h

Abstract:

    Header file for the debug tracing related function defintions and macros.

Environment:

    Kernel mode

--*/

//
// Define the tracing flags.
//
// Tracing GUID - d14c17c6-7e06-4452-82f1-c3d28f6559d0
//

#define WPP_CONTROL_GUIDS                                              \
    WPP_DEFINE_CONTROL_GUID(                                           \
        EtwDriverTraceGuid, (d14c17c6,7e06,4452,82f1,c3d28f6559d0), \
                                                                            \
        WPP_DEFINE_BIT(MYDRIVER_ALL_INFO)                              \
        WPP_DEFINE_BIT(TRACE_DRIVER)                                   \
        WPP_DEFINE_BIT(TRACE_DEVICE)                                   \
        WPP_DEFINE_BIT(TRACE_QUEUE)                                    \
        )                             

#define WPP_FLAG_LEVEL_LOGGER(flag, level)                                  \
    WPP_LEVEL_LOGGER(flag)

#define WPP_FLAG_LEVEL_ENABLED(flag, level)                                 \
    (WPP_LEVEL_ENABLED(flag) &&                                             \
     WPP_CONTROL(WPP_BIT_ ## flag).Level >= level)

#define WPP_LEVEL_FLAGS_LOGGER(lvl,flags) \
           WPP_LEVEL_LOGGER(flags)
               
#define WPP_LEVEL_FLAGS_ENABLED(lvl, flags) \
           (WPP_LEVEL_ENABLED(flags) && WPP_CONTROL(WPP_BIT_ ## flags).Level >= lvl)

//           
// WPP orders static parameters before dynamic parameters. To support the Trace function
// defined below which sets FLAGS=MYDRIVER_ALL_INFO, a custom macro must be defined to
// reorder the arguments to what the .tpl configuration file expects.
//
#define WPP_RECORDER_FLAGS_LEVEL_ARGS(flags, lvl) WPP_RECORDER_LEVEL_FLAGS_ARGS(lvl, flags)
#define WPP_RECORDER_FLAGS_LEVEL_FILTER(flags, lvl) WPP_RECORDER_LEVEL_FLAGS_FILTER(lvl, flags)

//
// This comment block is scanned by the trace preprocessor to define our
// Trace function.
//
// begin_wpp config
// FUNC Trace{FLAGS=MYDRIVER_ALL_INFO}(LEVEL, MSG, ...);
// FUNC TraceEvents(LEVEL, FLAGS, MSG, ...);
// end_wpp
//

```

`EtwDriver/EtwDriver/Worker.cpp`:

```cpp
#include "Worker.h"
#include "Worker.tmh"

volatile LONG g_PendingWorkItems = 0;

void SendMessageWorkItem(WDFWORKITEM workitem) {
	PSEND_MESSAGE_CONTEXT ctx = GetSendMessageContext(workitem);

	NTSTATUS status = SendMessage(ctx->msg); 

	if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) { 
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "SendMessage failed %!STATUS!", status); 
	}

	WdfObjectDelete(workitem);
}

// Queue message in worker pool
NTSTATUS EnqueueMessage(const Message& msg) {
	NTSTATUS status = STATUS_SUCCESS;
	WDFWORKITEM workitem = nullptr;

	if (g_WorkerDevice == nullptr) {
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "g_WorkerDevice is nullptr");
		return STATUS_DEVICE_NOT_READY;
	}

	LONG depth = InterlockedIncrement(&g_PendingWorkItems);
	if (depth > MAX_PENDING_WORK_ITEMS) {
		InterlockedDecrement(&g_PendingWorkItems);
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_WARNING, TRACE_DRIVER,
			"Queue full (%ld pending), dropping event tag=%d", depth, (int)msg.tag);
		return STATUS_INSUFFICIENT_RESOURCES;
	}


	WDF_OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES attributes;
	WDF_OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES_INIT_CONTEXT_TYPE(&attributes, SEND_MESSAGE_CONTEXT);

	attributes.ParentObject = g_WorkerDevice;

	WDF_WORKITEM_CONFIG config;
	WDF_WORKITEM_CONFIG_INIT(&config, SendMessageWorkItem);

	config.AutomaticSerialization = FALSE;

	status = WdfWorkItemCreate(&config, &attributes, &workitem);

	if (!NT_SUCCESS(status)) {
		TraceEvents(TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR, TRACE_DRIVER, "WdfWorkItemCreate failed. Status: %!STATUS!", status);
		return status;
	}

	PSEND_MESSAGE_CONTEXT ctx = GetSendMessageContext(workitem);

	ctx->msg = msg;

	WdfWorkItemEnqueue(workitem);

	return STATUS_SUCCESS;

}
```

`EtwDriver/EtwDriver/Worker.h`:

```h
#pragma once
#include <ntddk.h>
#include <wdf.h>
#include "Comms.h"

extern WDFDEVICE g_WorkerDevice;


typedef struct _SEND_MESSAGE_CONTEXT {
	Message msg;

} SEND_MESSAGE_CONTEXT, *PSEND_MESSAGE_CONTEXT;

WDF_DECLARE_CONTEXT_TYPE_WITH_NAME(SEND_MESSAGE_CONTEXT, GetSendMessageContext)

constexpr LONG MAX_PENDING_WORK_ITEMS = 512;

extern volatile LONG g_PendingWorkItems;

void SendMessageWorkItem(WDFWORKITEM workitem);
NTSTATUS EnqueueMessage(const Message& msg);

```

`Include/AlertContainer.hh`:

```hh
#ifndef EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_ALERTCONTAINER_HH
#define EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_ALERTCONTAINER_HH
#include <array>
#include <ctime>
#include <ranges>
#include <shared_mutex>
#include <span>
#include <string>
#include <vector>

#include "ObserverManager.hh"

  std::string title;
  std::string text;
  std::time_t timestamp;
  unsigned int process_id;
};

class IAlertObserver {
public:
  virtual ~IAlertObserver() = default;
  //required
  virtual void OnAlert(const Alert& alert) = 0;
};


class AlertContainer : public ObserverManager<IAlertObserver> {
public:
  ~AlertContainer() override = default;
  AlertContainer(const AlertContainer&) = delete;
  AlertContainer& operator=(const AlertContainer&) = delete;

  AlertContainer(AlertContainer&&) = delete;
  AlertContainer& operator=(AlertContainer&&) = delete;

  void InsertAlert(const Alert& alert);
  static AlertContainer& GetInstance();

private:
  AlertContainer() = default;
};
```

`Include/Config.hh`:

```hh
//
// Created by dev on 3/3/2026.
//

#ifndef EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_CONFIG_HH
#define EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_CONFIG_HH
#include <optional>
#include <string>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <variant>

using config_type = std::variant<std::string, int, bool>;

class Config {
public:
  template <typename T>
  std::optional<T> Get(std::string config_name) {
    if (config_.empty())
      return std::nullopt;

    auto item = std::get_if<T>(&config_[config_name]);

    if (item == nullptr)
      return std::nullopt;

    return *item;
  }

  template <typename T>
  bool Set(std::string config_name, T&& config_value) {
    if (config_.contains(config_name))
      return false;

    config_[config_name] = std::forward<T>(config_value);
    return true;
  }

  template <typename T>
  bool Reset(std::string config_name, T&& config_value) {
    if (!Exists(config_name))
      return false;

    config_[config_name] = std::forward<T>(config_value);
    return true;
  }

  bool Exists(const std::string& config_value) const;
  bool FromJson();
private:
  std::unordered_map<std::string, config_type> config_;
};




#endif //EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_CONFIG_HH
```

`Include/Messages.hh`:

```hh
#ifndef EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_MESSAGES_HH
#define EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_MESSAGES_HH
#include <windows.h>
#include <ctime>
#include <Types.hh>

struct ProcessCreation {
  LARGE_INTEGER creation_time;
  unsigned int process_id;
};

struct ProcessExit {
  unsigned int process_id;
};

struct ThreadCreation {
  LARGE_INTEGER creation_time;
  unsigned int process_id;
  unsigned int thread_id;
};

struct ThreadExit {
  unsigned int process_id;
  unsigned int thread_id;
};

struct ImageLoadEvt {
  LARGE_INTEGER load_time;
  unsigned int process_id;
  unsigned int thread_id;
  ImageLoad image_load;
};

enum class Tag {
  ProcessCreation = 0,
  ProcessExit = 1,
  ThreadCreation = 2,
  ThreadExit = 3,
  ImageLoad = 4,
};

struct Message {
  Tag tag;
  // only matching Tag can be used.
  union {
    ProcessCreation creation;
    ProcessExit exit;
    ThreadCreation thread_creation;
    ThreadExit thread_exit;
    ImageLoadEvt image_load;
  };
};

#endif  // EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_MESSAGES_HH

```

`Include/ObserverManager.hh`:

```hh
#ifndef EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_OBSERVERMANAGER_HH
#define EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_OBSERVERMANAGER_HH
#include <memory>
#include <shared_mutex>
#include <vector>

template <typename ObserverType>
class ObserverManager {
public:
  virtual ~ObserverManager() = default;
  /**
   * @brief Registers a new observer
   * @param observer shared_ptr to ObserverType
   * @return false if observer is nullptr, true if its not
   */
  bool RegisterObserver(
      std::shared_ptr<ObserverType> observer) {
    std::unique_lock lock(mutex_);

    if (observer == nullptr) {
      return false;
    }

    observers_.push_back(observer);
    return true;
  }

  /**
   * @brief Get pointer to stored observer object
   * @tparam T Observer type
   * @return returns a shared pointer of the derived observer
   */
  template <typename T>
  std::shared_ptr<T> GetObserver() {
      std::shared_lock lock(mutex_);
      for (auto& observer : observers_) {
        if ( auto observer_ptr = std::dynamic_pointer_cast<T>(observer) ) {
          return observer_ptr;
        }
      }
      return nullptr;
  }
  /**
   * @brief Unregisters an observer
   * @param observer shared_ptr to ObserverType
   * @return true if unregistered, false if not.
   */
  bool UnregisterObserver(
      std::shared_ptr<ObserverType> observer) {
    std::unique_lock lock(mutex_);

    if (observer == nullptr) {
      return false;
    }

    auto it =
      std::find(observers_.begin(), observers_.end(), observer);

    if (it != observers_.end()) {
      observers_.erase(it);
      return true;
    }
    return false;
  }

protected:
  std::shared_mutex mutex_;
  std::vector<std::shared_ptr<ObserverType>> observers_;
};

#endif //EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_OBSERVERMANAGER_HH

```

`Include/Util.hh`:

```hh
#ifndef EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_UTIL_HH
#define EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_UTIL_HH
#include <windows.h>

#include <array>
#include <bit>
#include <cstring>
#include <sstream>
#include <string>

bool GuidCompare(const GUID& guid1, const GUID& guid2);
std::time_t LargeIntToTimeT(const LARGE_INTEGER time);

namespace std {
  template<> struct hash<GUID> {
    size_t operator()(const GUID& guid) const noexcept {
      size_t hash = 0;
      const auto t = std::bit_cast<std::array<uint8_t, sizeof(GUID)>>(guid);

      for (size_t i = 0; i < 16; ++i) {
        hash ^= t[i] + 0x9e3779b9 + (hash << 6) + (hash >> 2);
      }
      return hash;
    }
  };
}

#endif //EYYOETWWHEREYOUAT_UTIL_HH
```

`Ipc.cc`:

```cc
#include <Ipc.hh>

/**
 * @brief ctor Sets up the namedpipe
 * @param pipe_name unicode string for the named pipe name
 * @throws runtime error if namedpipe fails to create
 */
Ipc::Ipc(std::wstring pipe_name) : pipe_name_(std::move(pipe_name)) {
  // @TODO add SD
  pipe_handle_ = CreateNamedPipeW(pipe_name_.data(),
    PIPE_ACCESS_DUPLEX,
    PIPE_TYPE_MESSAGE | PIPE_READMODE_MESSAGE | PIPE_WAIT,
    PIPE_UNLIMITED_INSTANCES,
    512,
    512,
    0,
    nullptr);

  if (pipe_handle_ == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
    throw std::runtime_error("Ipc::Ipc: pipe creation failed");
  }
}

/**
 * @brief Cleans up on object destruction
 */
Ipc::~Ipc() {
  if (pipe_handle_ != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
    Stop();
    CloseHandle(pipe_handle_);
  }
}

/**
 * @brief Starts listening on the named pipe.
 */
void Ipc::Listen()
{
  while (is_running_) {
    auto connected = ConnectNamedPipe(pipe_handle_, nullptr);

    if ( connected || (GetLastError() == ERROR_PIPE_CONNECTED) )
    {
      HANDLE client_pipe = pipe_handle_;
      try {
        std::thread t(&Ipc::ClientHandler, client_pipe);
        t.detach();//yolo
      }catch (const std::exception& e) {
        std::cerr << e.what() << std::endl;
      }
      //@TODO Fix permissions
      pipe_handle_ = CreateNamedPipeW(pipe_name_.data(),
                            PIPE_ACCESS_DUPLEX,
                            PIPE_TYPE_MESSAGE | PIPE_READMODE_MESSAGE | PIPE_WAIT,
                            PIPE_UNLIMITED_INSTANCES,
                            512,
                            512,
                            0,
                            nullptr);

      if (pipe_handle_ == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
        throw std::runtime_error("Ipc::Listen: pipe creation failed");
      }

    } else {
      break;
    }
  }
}

/**
 * @brief stops the IPC
 */
void Ipc::Stop()
{
  is_running_ = false;
  CancelIoEx(pipe_handle_, nullptr);
}

/**
 * @brief Handles individually connected clients
 * @param hPipe HANDLE to named pipe
 */
void Ipc::ClientHandler(const HANDLE hPipe) {
  DWORD bytes_read = 0;
  char buffer[sizeof(Message)];

  while (true) {
    bool success = ReadFile(hPipe, buffer, sizeof(buffer), &bytes_read, nullptr);

    if (!success)
    {
      DWORD error = GetLastError();
      if (error == ERROR_MORE_DATA) {
        continue;
      } else {
        break;
      }
    }

    if ( bytes_read > 0 && bytes_read >= sizeof(Message) ) {
      const auto message = reinterpret_cast<Message*>(buffer);
      ParseMessage(message);
    }
  }

  DisconnectNamedPipe(hPipe);
  CloseHandle(hPipe);
}

/**
 * @brief Parses IPC response from Kernel event callbacks
 * @param message Message type received from the kernel event.
 */
void Ipc::ParseMessage(const Message* message) {
  auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();

  switch (message->tag) {
    case Tag::ImageLoad: {
        storage.InsertImageLoad(
          message->image_load.process_id,
          message->image_load.thread_id,
          message->image_load.image_load
          );
        break;
    }
    case Tag::ProcessCreation: {

      storage.InsertProcess(
          message->creation.process_id,
          LargeIntToTimeT(message->creation.creation_time)
          );
        break;
    }
    case Tag::ProcessExit: {
      storage.RemoveProcess(message->exit.process_id);
        break;
    }
    case Tag::ThreadExit: {
      storage.RemoveThread(
          message->thread_exit.process_id,
          message->thread_exit.thread_id
          );
        break;
    }
    case Tag::ThreadCreation: {
        storage.InsertThread(
            message->thread_creation.process_id,
            message->thread_creation.thread_id,
            LargeIntToTimeT(message->thread_creation.creation_time)
            );
        break;
    }
    default:
      break;
  }
}
```

```cc
//
// Created by DEV on 1/23/2026.

#include <Logger.hh>


/**
 * @brief Returns the singleton instance of this class
 * @note Thread-safe if compiled with C++11 or later (magic statics)
 * @return Reference to the single static instance
 */
Logger& Logger::GetInstance() {
  static Logger instance;
  return instance;
}

/**
 * @brief Logs a ascii string
 * @param str string to send to all registered observers
 */
void Logger::Logln(const std::string_view str) const {
  for (const auto& observer : observers_) {
    observer->Logln(str);
  }
}

/**
 * @brief Logs a unicode string
 * @param str wstring to send to all registered observers
 */
void Logger::Logln(const std::wstring_view str) const {
  for (const auto& observer : observers_) {
    observer->Logln(str);
  }
}
```

`Process.cc`:

```cc
#include <Process.hh>


/**
 * @brief Inserts a new thread into the threads map
 * @param thread_id The unique identifier for the thread
 * @param creation_time Timestamp at which the thread was created
 * @return Boolean
 */
bool Process::InsertThread(const unsigned int thread_id,
                          const std::time_t creation_time) {
  if (threads_.contains(thread_id)) {
    return false;
  }

  threads_.emplace(thread_id, creation_time);
  return true;
}

/**
 * @brief Removes thread with thread_id identifier
 * @param thread_id The unique identifier for the thread
 * @return true if removes, false if doesn't exist.
 */
bool Process::RemoveThread(const unsigned int thread_id) {
  if (!threads_.contains(thread_id)) {
    return false;
  }

  return threads_.erase(thread_id);
}

/**
 * @brief Gets an individual thread object by id
 * @param thread_id The unique identifier for the thread
 * @return Thread if thread_id exists, nullptr if it doesn't
 */
const Thread* Process::GetThreadById(const unsigned int thread_id) const
{
  if (const auto& it = threads_.find(thread_id); it != threads_.end()) {
    return &(it->second);
  }

  return nullptr;
}

/**
 * @brief  Gets reference to all threads
 * @return unordered_map returns all threads with thread id and Thread Object.
 */
const std::unordered_map<unsigned int, Thread>& Process::GetThreads() const
{
  return threads_;
}

/**
 * @brief Inserts an imageload
 * @param image_load The unique identifier for the image load.
 * @return boolean Returns true if the image was inserted, false if it didnt exist.
 * @TODO Actually get the iterator from insert and return ->second
 */
bool Process::InsertImageLoad(const ImageLoad image_load, unsigned int tid) {
  if (images_.contains(image_load)) {
    return false;
  }

  if (const auto it = threads_.find(tid); it != threads_.end()) {
    it->second.InsertImageLoad(image_load);
  }

  auto [fst, snd] = images_.insert(image_load);
  return snd;
}

/**
 * @brief Removes an image load, if an image is free'd during execution.
 * @param image_load The unique identifier for the image load.
 * @return boolean Returns true if the image was removed, false if it didnt exist.
 */
bool Process::RemoveImageLoad(const ImageLoad image_load) {
  if (images_.contains(image_load) == false) {
    return false;
  }

  images_.erase(image_load);
  return true;
}
/**
 * @brief Increments the counter by 1 for a thread under the given image load.
 * @param image_load The unique identifier for the image load.
 * @param tid The unique identifier for the thread
 */
void Process::IncrementEventCount(const ImageLoad image_load, const unsigned int tid) {
    if (const auto it = threads_.find(tid); it != threads_.end()) {
      it->second.IncrementCount(image_load);
    }
}

/**
 * @brief
 * @return returns an unordered_set of ImageLoad, which stores any DLL Loads the process has.
 */
const std::unordered_set<ImageLoad>& Process::GetImageLoads() const
{
  return images_;
}

/**
 * @brief Returns the time at which the process was created
 * @return time_t returns creation_time_ time process was created
 */
std::time_t Process::GetCreationTime() const {
  return creation_time_;
}

/**
 * @brief Gets the total number of threads
 * @return int number of threads
 */
unsigned int Process::GetThreadCount() const {
  return threads_.size();
}

/**
 * @brief Creates a new process object
 * @param creation_time Timestamp at which the thread was created
 */
Process::Process(const std::time_t creation_time) {
  creation_time_ = creation_time;
}
```

`README.md`:

```md
# EyYoEtwWhereYouAt

Proof of concept tool that monitors kernel events (image loads, process creation, thread creation) and identifies anomalous absences in corresponding ETW telemetry. When system activity occurs without expected ETW events, IE ETW Patching.

It has one very obvious bypass in that you could hook EtwWriteEvent or NtTraceEvent and just modify some of the event data and send it on it's way. Possible work around for that would be to create a database of events that should exist hash any that can be hashed and match against them from the ETW consumeer.

Whilst this is effective at detecting ETW patching it does have some FPs still, the analysis could be improved significantly.

FPs generally are processes that spend a lot of time waiting, increasing the time between analysis or even logging the last X cycles or something could be better.

### Prerequisites
- Administrative privileges on the system
- Secure boot disabled
- Driver test signing enabled
- CMake
- MSVC 2022 (2026 isn't compatible with drivers currently)
- Virtual Machine - a must, this is a PoC.

### Compilation
```

```
### Usage

- Install driver with `sc.exe create EtwDriver type= kernel binPath=C:\path\to\driver`
- Run compiled exe as local administrator.
- Start driver `sc.exe start EtwDriver`
- Run application with ETW Patching.

### Notes: 
- Driver might crash, it was the first time I wrote a driver.
- Some unused code as I was going to make this a larger project but decided against it.
- May have some FPs, I didnt do too much in the analysis "engine" could be improved.
- I made some refactoring and didn't bother updating the unit tests
```

`Storage.cc`:

```cc
#include <Storage.hh>

/**
 * @brief Returns the singleton instance of this class
 * @note Thread-safe if compiled with C++11 or later (magic statics)
 * @return Reference to the single static instance
 */
Storage& Storage::GetInstance() {
  static Storage instance;
  return instance;
}

/**
 * @brief Clears the process map.
 */
void Storage::Clear()
{
  std::unique_lock lock(processes_mutex_);
  processes_.clear();
}

/**
 * @brief Inserts a process into the process map.
 * @param pid The unique identifier for the process
 * @param creation_time creation time of the process
 */
bool Storage::InsertProcess(const unsigned int pid, const std::time_t creation_time) {
  std::unique_lock lock(processes_mutex_);

  if (processes_.contains(pid) == false) {
    const auto [fst, snd] = processes_.emplace(pid, creation_time);
    return snd;
  }

  return false;
}
/**
 * @brief Removes a process from the process map
 * @param pid The unique identifier for the process
 */
bool Storage::RemoveProcess(const unsigned int pid) {
  std::unique_lock lock(processes_mutex_);

  if (processes_.contains(pid) == true) {
    return static_cast<bool>(processes_.erase(pid));
  }

  return false;
}
/**
 * @brief Check if the process id exists in the map
 * @param pid The unique identifier for the process
 * @return true if exists, false if doesn't
 */
bool Storage::HasProcess(const unsigned int pid) const {
  std::shared_lock read_lock(processes_mutex_);
  return processes_.contains(pid);
}

/**
 * @brief Check if thread id exists within a process
 * @param pid The unique identifier for the process
 * @param tid The unique identifier for the theread
 * @return true if exists, false if doesn't
 */
bool Storage::HasThread(const unsigned int pid, const unsigned int tid) const {
  std::shared_lock read_lock(processes_mutex_);

  if (auto it = processes_.find(pid); it != processes_.end()) {
    return (it->second.GetThreadById(tid) != nullptr);
  }

  return false;
}

/**
 * @brief Retrieves a process from the process map by PID
 * @param pid The process identifier to look up
 * @return Pointer to the matching Process, or nullptr if not found
 */
const Process* Storage::GetProcess(const unsigned int pid) const
{
  std::shared_lock read_lock(processes_mutex_);

  if (const auto it = processes_.find(pid); it != processes_.end()) {
    return &(it->second);
  }

  return nullptr;
}
/**
 * @brief Gets all processes
 * @return returns a copy of all processes.
 */
std::unordered_map<unsigned int, Process> Storage::GetProcesses() const {
  std::shared_lock read_lock(processes_mutex_);

  return processes_;
}

/**
 * @brief Insert a thread into a process by id
 * @param pid The unique identifier for the process
 * @param tid The unique identifier for the thread
 * @param creation_time creation time of the process
 */
bool Storage::InsertThread(const unsigned int pid, const unsigned int tid,
                           const std::time_t creation_time) {
  std::unique_lock lock(processes_mutex_);
  if (auto it = processes_.find(pid); it != processes_.end()) {
    return it->second.InsertThread(tid, creation_time);
  }
  return false;
}
/**
 * @brief Removes a thread from a process by id
 * @param pid The unique identifier for the process
 * @param tid The unique identifier for the thread
 */
bool Storage::RemoveThread(const unsigned int pid, const unsigned int tid) {
  bool result = false;
  {
    std::unique_lock lock(processes_mutex_);
    if (auto it = processes_.find(pid); it != processes_.end()) {
      if ( it->second.RemoveThread(tid) ) {
        result = true;
      }
    }
  }// lock is released
  if (on_thread_exit_) on_thread_exit_(tid);

  return result;
}


/**
 * @brief Inserts an imageload into a given process
 * @param pid The unique identifier for the process
 * @param image_load
 */
bool Storage::InsertImageLoad(const unsigned int pid, const unsigned int tid, const ImageLoad image_load) {
  std::unique_lock lock(processes_mutex_);

  if (const auto it = processes_.find(pid); it != processes_.end()) {
    return it->second.InsertImageLoad(image_load, tid);
  }

  return false;
}
/**
 * @brief Removes an imageload into a given process
 * @param pid The unique identifier for the process
 * @param image_load
 */
bool Storage::RemoveImageLoad(const unsigned int pid, const ImageLoad image_load) {
  std::unique_lock lock(processes_mutex_);

    if ( const auto it = processes_.find(pid); it != processes_.end() ) {
      return it->second.RemoveImageLoad(image_load);
    }
  return false;
}

/**
 * @brief Increments the event counter for a thread for the given image.
 * @param image_load Image load can be Clr, WinHttp, WinInet
 * @param pid The unique identifier for the process
 * @param tid The unique identifier for the thread
 */
bool Storage::IncrementThreadEventCount(ImageLoad image_load, const unsigned int pid, const unsigned int tid) {
  std::unique_lock lock(processes_mutex_);

  if (const auto& it = processes_.find(pid); it != processes_.end()) {
    it->second.IncrementEventCount(image_load, tid);
    return true;
  }
  return false;
}

/**
 * @brief Get number of processes
 * @return count of processes
 */
unsigned int Storage::GetProcessCount() const {
  std::shared_lock read_lock(processes_mutex_);
  return processes_.size();
}

/**
 * @brief Sets a callback that gets executed when RemoveThread is called.
 * @param on_thread_exit function pointer to call on thread removal.
 */
void Storage::SetThreadExitCallback(
    const std::function<void(unsigned int)>& on_thread_exit) {
  on_thread_exit_ = on_thread_exit;
}
```

`Test/Ipc_Test.cc`:

```cc
#include "../Include/Ipc.hh"

#include <catch2/catch_test_macros.hpp>
#include <iostream>

#include "../Include/Messages.hh"

class IpcTest {
public:
  IpcTest(const std::wstring& pipe_name) : ipc_(pipe_name), pipe_name_(pipe_name)  {
    listener_ = std::thread([this]() {
      try {
        ipc_.Listen();
      }catch (const std::exception& e) {
        std::cerr << e.what() << std::endl;
      }
    });
    std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::milliseconds(200));
  }
  ~IpcTest() {
    ipc_.Stop();
    if (listener_.joinable()) {
      listener_.join();
    }
  }

  void SendMessage(const Message& msg) const {
    HANDLE client = CreateFileW(pipe_name_.c_str(),
  GENERIC_WRITE,
  0,
  nullptr,
  OPEN_EXISTING,
  0,
  nullptr);

    if (client == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
      throw std::runtime_error("Failed to connect to pipe");
    }

    DWORD bytesWritten = 0;
    BOOL result = WriteFile(client, &msg, sizeof(msg), &bytesWritten, nullptr);
    CloseHandle(client);

    if (!result || bytesWritten != sizeof(msg)) {
      throw std::runtime_error("Failed to send message");
    }

    std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::milliseconds(100));
  }

  void CreateProcess(unsigned int pid, std::time_t creation_time) const {
    Message msg {};
    msg.tag = Tag::ProcessCreation;
    msg.creation.process_id = pid;
    msg.creation.creation_time = creation_time;

    SendMessage(msg);
  }

  void ExitProcess(unsigned int pid) const {
    Message msg{};
    msg.tag = Tag::ProcessExit;
    msg.exit.process_id = pid;
  }
  void CreateThread(const unsigned int pid,
    const unsigned int tid,
    const std::time_t creation_time) {

    Message msg{};
    msg.tag = Tag::ThreadCreation;
    msg.thread_creation.process_id = pid;
    msg.thread_creation.creation_time = creation_time;
    msg.thread_creation.thread_id = tid;
    SendMessage(msg);
  }
  void ExitThread(unsigned int pid) const{}

  void ImageLoad(const unsigned int pid, const ImageLoad load) const {
    Message msg{};
    msg.tag = Tag::ImageLoad;
    msg.image_load.process_id = pid;
    msg.image_load.image_load = load;
    SendMessage(msg);
  }


private:
  Ipc ipc_;
  std::wstring pipe_name_;
  std::thread listener_;
};

TEST_CASE("IPC Initialization", "[IPC]"){
    REQUIRE_NOTHROW([]() {
      Ipc IPC(L"\\\\.\\pipe\\etw");
    }());
}
TEST_CASE("IPC bad Initialization", "[IPC]"){
  REQUIRE_THROWS([]() {
    Ipc IPC(L"asdfasdfa");
  }());
}
TEST_CASE("IPC Pipe exists", "[IPC]"){
    Ipc IPC(L"\\\\.\\pipe\\etw");

    HANDLE hPipe = CreateFileW(L"\\\\.\\pipe\\etw",
      GENERIC_READ,
      0,
      nullptr,
      OPEN_EXISTING,
      0,
      nullptr);

    REQUIRE(hPipe != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE);
    CloseHandle(hPipe);
}
// Create Process tests
TEST_CASE("IPC Pipe MessageParsing Tag::CreateProcess", "[IPC]")
{
  IpcTest fixture(L"\\\\.\\pipe\\etw");

  Message msg {};
  msg.tag = Tag::ProcessCreation;
  msg.creation.process_id = 1234;
  msg.creation.creation_time = std::time(nullptr);

  fixture.SendMessage(msg);

  auto& store = Storage::GetInstance();

  auto procs = store.GetProcesses();

  REQUIRE(procs.contains(1234) == true);
  store.Clear();
}
// Image load tests
TEST_CASE("IPC Pipe MessageParsing Tag::ImageLoad","[IPC]") {
  const IpcTest fixture(L"\\\\.\\pipe\\etw");

  auto pid = 1234u;

  fixture.CreateProcess(pid, std::time(nullptr));

  auto& store = Storage::GetInstance();

  auto procs = store.GetProcesses();

  REQUIRE(procs.contains(pid) == true);

  fixture.ImageLoad(pid, ImageLoad::WinHTTP);
}


// ExitProcess tests
TEST_CASE("IPC Pipe MessageParsing Tag::ProcessExit" , "[IPC]"){}


TEST_CASE("IPC Pipe MessageParsing Tag::ThreadExit", "[IPC]"){}
TEST_CASE("IPC Pipe MessageParsing Tag::ThreadCreation", "[IPC]"){}
```

`Test/ObserverManager_Test.cc`:

```cc
#include "../Include/ObserverManager.hh"

#include <catch2/catch_test_macros.hpp>

class ITestObserver {
public:
    virtual ~ITestObserver() = default;
    virtual int GetId() = 0;
};

class TestObserver : public ITestObserver {
public:
  int GetId() override {
    return 1;
  }
};

class TestObserver2 : public ITestObserver {
public:
  int GetId() override {
    return 1;
  }
};

class TestObserverManager : public ObserverManager<ITestObserver> {
  public:
  size_t GetObserverCount() {
    std::shared_lock lock(mutex_);
    return observers_.size();
  }
};

TEST_CASE("RegisterObserver", "[ObserverManager]") {
  TestObserverManager manager;
  SECTION("RegisterObserver") {
    REQUIRE(manager.RegisterObserver(std::make_shared<TestObserver>()) == true);
    REQUIRE(manager.GetObserverCount() == 1);
  }
  SECTION("RegisterObserver -- nullptr") {
    REQUIRE(manager.RegisterObserver(nullptr) == false);
  }

  SECTION("RegisterObserver -- multiple different observers") {
    REQUIRE(manager.RegisterObserver(std::make_shared<TestObserver2>()) == true);
    REQUIRE(manager.RegisterObserver(std::make_shared<TestObserver>()) == true);
    REQUIRE(manager.GetObserverCount() == 2);
  }

  SECTION("RegisterObserver -- multiple different observers") {
    REQUIRE(manager.RegisterObserver(std::make_shared<TestObserver>()) == true);
    REQUIRE(manager.RegisterObserver(std::make_shared<TestObserver>()) == true);
    REQUIRE(manager.GetObserverCount() == 2);
  }
}
TEST_CASE("UnregisterObserver", "[ObserverManager]") {
  TestObserverManager manager;
  auto observer = std::make_shared<TestObserver>();

  SECTION("UnregisterObserver -- default use-case") {
    REQUIRE(manager.RegisterObserver(observer) == true);
    REQUIRE(manager.GetObserverCount() == 1);
    REQUIRE(manager.UnregisterObserver(observer) == true);
    REQUIRE(manager.GetObserverCount() == 0);
  }
  SECTION("UnregisterObserver -- nullptr") {
    REQUIRE(manager.UnregisterObserver(nullptr) == false);
  }

  SECTION("UnregisterObserver -- Non-existent observer") {
    REQUIRE(manager.UnregisterObserver(observer) == false);
  }
  SECTION("UnregisterObserver -- multiple observers - only removes first matching") {
    REQUIRE(manager.RegisterObserver(observer) == true);
    REQUIRE(manager.RegisterObserver(observer) == true);
    REQUIRE(manager.GetObserverCount() == 2);
    REQUIRE(manager.UnregisterObserver(observer) == true);
    REQUIRE(manager.GetObserverCount() == 1);
  }

  SECTION("UnregisterObserver -- unregister empty container") {
    REQUIRE(manager.UnregisterObserver(observer) == false);
  }
}
TEST_CASE("GetObserver", "[ObserverManager]") {
  TestObserverManager manager;
  manager.RegisterObserver(std::make_shared<TestObserver2>());

  SECTION("No observers registered") {
    REQUIRE(manager.GetObserver<TestObserver>() == nullptr);
  }

  SECTION("No type observers registered") {
    REQUIRE(manager.GetObserver<TestObserver>() == nullptr);
  }

  SECTION("return registered observer") {
    auto obs = manager.GetObserver<TestObserver2>();
    REQUIRE(obs != nullptr);
  }

}
```

```cc
#include "../Include/Process.hh"

#include <catch2/catch_test_macros.hpp>

TEST_CASE("Process Initialization", "[PROCESS]") {
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);

  const Process pr(start);

  REQUIRE(pr.GetCreationTime() == start);
}
TEST_CASE("Process Initialization thread count is 0", "[PROCESS]") {
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);

  const Process pr(start);

  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 0);
}

// thread tests
TEST_CASE("Process insert thread", "[PROCESS]")
{
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);
  Process pr(start);
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 0);
  pr.InsertThread(1000u, std::time(nullptr));
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 1);
}
TEST_CASE("Process insert thread already exists", "[PROCESS]")
{
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);
  Process pr(start);
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 0);
  pr.InsertThread(1000u, std::time(nullptr));
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 1);
  REQUIRE(pr.InsertThread(1000u, std::time(nullptr)) == false);
}

TEST_CASE("Process remove thread", "[PROCESS]")
{
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);

  constexpr auto tid = 1000u;

  Process pr(start);
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 0);
  pr.InsertThread(tid, std::time(nullptr));
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 1);
  pr.RemoveThread(tid);
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 0);
}
TEST_CASE("Process remove thread doesn't exist", "[PROCESS]")
{
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);
  Process pr(start);

  REQUIRE(pr.RemoveThread(101u) == false);
}

TEST_CASE("Process get thread by Id", "[PROCESS]")
{
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);

  constexpr auto tid = 1000u;

  Process pr(start);
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 0);
  pr.InsertThread(tid, start);
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 1);

  auto thread = pr.GetThreadById(tid);
  REQUIRE(thread->GetCreationTime() == start);
}
TEST_CASE("Process get thread by Id doesn't exist", "[PROCESS]")
{
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);

  constexpr auto tid = 1000u;

  Process pr(start);
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 0);
  pr.InsertThread(tid, start);
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 1);

  auto thread = pr.GetThreadById(1001u);
  REQUIRE(thread == nullptr);
}


TEST_CASE("Process get all threads", "[PROCESS]")
{
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);

  Process pr(start);
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 0);
  pr.InsertThread(100u, std::time(nullptr));
  pr.InsertThread(101u, std::time(nullptr));
  pr.InsertThread(102u, std::time(nullptr));

  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 3);

  auto threads = pr.GetThreads();
  REQUIRE(threads.size() == 3);
}
TEST_CASE("Process increment thread count", "[PROCESS]")
{
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);

  constexpr auto tid = 1000u;

  Process pr(start);
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 0);
  pr.InsertThread(tid, std::time(nullptr));
  REQUIRE(pr.GetThreadCount() == 1);

  pr.IncrementEventCount(tid);
  auto thread = pr.GetThreadById(tid);

  REQUIRE(thread->GetEventCount() == 1);

}


// image load insertion
TEST_CASE("Process Insert image load", "[PROCESS]")
{
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);

  constexpr auto tid = 1000;

  Process pr(start);
  pr.InsertImageLoad(ImageLoad::WinHTTP);

  const auto image = pr.GetImageLoads();

  REQUIRE(image.contains(ImageLoad::WinHTTP) == 1);
}
TEST_CASE("Process Insert image load already exists", "[PROCESS]")

  constexpr auto tid = 1000;

  Process pr(start);
  pr.InsertImageLoad(ImageLoad::WinHTTP);
  REQUIRE(pr.InsertImageLoad(ImageLoad::WinHTTP) == false);
}


// image load removal

TEST_CASE("Process remove image load", "[PROCESS]"){
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);

  constexpr auto tid = 1000;

  Process pr(start);
  pr.InsertImageLoad(ImageLoad::WinHTTP);
  REQUIRE(pr.RemoveImageLoad(ImageLoad::WinHTTP) == true);
}
TEST_CASE("Process remove image load non-existing", "[PROCESS]"){
  const std::time_t start = std::time(nullptr);

  constexpr auto tid = 1000;

  Process pr(start);

  REQUIRE(pr.RemoveImageLoad(ImageLoad::WinHTTP) == false);
}
```

`Test/Storage_Test.cc`:

```cc
#include "../Include/Storage.hh"

#include <catch2/catch_test_macros.hpp>

TEST_CASE("Basic functionality", "[STORAGE]") {
  SECTION("Singleton same instance") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    auto& storage2 = Storage::GetInstance();

    REQUIRE(&storage == &storage2);
  }
  SECTION("Singleton no copy") {
    static_assert(!std::is_copy_constructible_v<Storage>,
              "Storage should not be copy constructible");
    static_assert(!std::is_copy_assignable_v<Storage>,
                  "Storage should not be copy assignable");
    SUCCEED("Copy operations are properly deleted");
  }
}

TEST_CASE("Process management", "[STORAGE]") {
  SECTION("Insert Process")
  {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time) == true);
    storage.Clear();
  }
  SECTION("Insert Process duplicate")
  {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();

    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);

    REQUIRE(storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time) == false);
    storage.Clear();
  }
  SECTION("Remove Process") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    constexpr auto pid2 = 502u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time) == true);

    REQUIRE(storage.RemoveProcess(pid) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.RemoveProcess(pid2) == false);
    storage.Clear();
  }
  SECTION("HasProcess") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    constexpr auto pid2 = 502u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.HasProcess(pid) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.HasProcess(pid2) == false);
    storage.Clear();
  }
  SECTION("GetProcess") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    constexpr auto pid2 = 502u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.HasProcess(pid) == true);

    auto proc = storage.GetProcess(pid);
    REQUIRE(proc != nullptr);
    REQUIRE(proc->GetCreationTime() == creation_time);

    REQUIRE(storage.GetProcess(pid2) == nullptr);

    storage.Clear();
  }
  SECTION("GetProcesses") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    constexpr auto pid2 = 502u;
    constexpr auto pid4 = 503u;
    constexpr auto pid5 = 504u;

    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertProcess(pid2, creation_time) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertProcess(pid4, creation_time) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertProcess(pid5, creation_time) == true);

    auto proc = storage.GetProcesses();

    REQUIRE(proc.contains(pid) == true);
    REQUIRE(proc.contains(pid2) == true);
    REQUIRE(proc.contains(pid4) == true);
    REQUIRE(proc.contains(pid5) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.GetProcessCount() == 4);
    storage.Clear();
  }
}

TEST_CASE("Thread Management", "[STORAGE]") {
  SECTION("Insert Thread to existing process") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time);

    constexpr auto tid = 1234u;
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertThread(pid, tid, creation_time) == true);


    storage.Clear();
  }
  SECTION("Insert Thread duplicate to existing process") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time);

    constexpr auto tid = 1234u;
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertThread(pid, tid, creation_time) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertThread(pid, tid, creation_time) == false);

    storage.Clear();
  }
  SECTION("Insert Thread to non-existing process") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    constexpr auto tid = 1234u;
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertThread(pid, tid, creation_time) == false);
    storage.Clear();
  }
  SECTION("Remove Thread") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    constexpr auto tid = 1234u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);

    storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time);
    storage.InsertThread(pid, tid, creation_time);
    REQUIRE(storage.GetProcess(pid)->GetThreadCount() == 1);
    REQUIRE(storage.RemoveThread(pid, tid) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.GetProcess(pid)->GetThreadCount() == 0);

    REQUIRE(storage.RemoveThread(pid, tid) == false);
    storage.Clear();
  }

  SECTION("Has Thread") {}
  SECTION("GetThread") {}
  SECTION("GetThreads") {}
}

TEST_CASE("Imageload Management", "[STORAGE]") {
  SECTION("Insert Imageload") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time);

    constexpr auto tid = 1234u;
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertThread(pid, tid, creation_time) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertImageLoad(pid, ImageLoad::Clr) == true);
    storage.Clear();
  }
  SECTION("Duplicate behaviour") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time);

    constexpr auto tid = 1234u;
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertThread(pid, tid, creation_time) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertImageLoad(pid, ImageLoad::Clr) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertImageLoad(pid, ImageLoad::Clr) == false);
    storage.Clear();
  }
  SECTION("Remove") {
    auto& storage = Storage::GetInstance();
    constexpr auto pid = 501u;
    const auto creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
    storage.InsertProcess(pid, creation_time);

    constexpr auto tid = 1234u;
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertThread(pid, tid, creation_time) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.InsertImageLoad(pid, ImageLoad::Clr) == true);

    REQUIRE(storage.RemoveImageLoad(pid, ImageLoad::Clr) == true);
    REQUIRE(storage.RemoveImageLoad(pid, ImageLoad::Clr) == false);

    storage.Clear();
  }
}

TEST_CASE("Event Incrementation", "[STORAGE]") {
  SECTION("Duplicate behaviour") {}
  SECTION("Remove") {}
}
```

```cc
#include "../Include/Thread.hh"

#include <catch2/catch_test_macros.hpp>

TEST_CASE("Basic Functionality", "[THREAD]") {
  const std::time_t creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
  const Thread tr(creation_time);

  REQUIRE(tr.GetEventCount() == 0);
  REQUIRE(tr.GetCreationTime() == creation_time);
}
TEST_CASE("Thread increment event count", "[THREAD]") {
  const std::time_t creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
  Thread tr(creation_time);

  tr.IncrementCount();

  REQUIRE(tr.GetEventCount() == 1);
}
TEST_CASE("Thread increment multiple event count", "[THREAD]") {
  const std::time_t creation_time = std::time(nullptr);
  Thread tr(creation_time);

  tr.IncrementCount();
  tr.IncrementCount();
  tr.IncrementCount();
  tr.IncrementCount();
  tr.IncrementCount();

  REQUIRE(tr.GetEventCount() == 5);
}
```

`Test/kernel_mock.cc`:

```cc
#include <windows.h>
#include <Messages.hh>
#include <print>
#include <random>

HANDLE g_ConnectionPort = nullptr;

unsigned int GenerateRandomNumber() {
  std::random_device rd;
  std::mt19937 gen(rd());
  std::uniform_int_distribution<unsigned int> dis(0, 255);
  return dis(gen);
}




bool WriteData(const Message &msg) {
  if ( g_ConnectionPort == nullptr ) {
    return false;
  }
  return WriteFile(g_ConnectionPort, &msg, sizeof(Message), nullptr, nullptr);
}

int main(int argc, char **argv) {
  g_ConnectionPort = CreateFile(
                    L"\\\\.\\pipe\\Etw",
                    GENERIC_WRITE,
                    0,
                    NULL,
                    OPEN_EXISTING,
                    0,
                    NULL);

  if ( g_ConnectionPort == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE ) {
    std::println(stderr, "CreateFile() failed with error {}", GetLastError());
    return 1;
  }

  Sleep(10000);
  auto pid = 0;
  auto tid = 0;

  while (true) {
    bool has_image_load = false;
    if ( argc != 3) {
      pid = GenerateRandomNumber();
      tid = GetCurrentThreadId();
    }else {
      pid = std::atoi(argv[1]);
      tid = std::atoi(argv[2]);
    }

    Message process{};
    process.tag = Tag::ProcessCreation;
    process.creation.process_id = pid;
    QueryPerformanceFrequency(&process.creation.creation_time);
    if ( ! WriteData(process)) {
      std::println(stderr, "WriteFile() failed with error {}", GetLastError());
    }

    Sleep(1000);

    Message thread{};
    thread.tag = Tag::ThreadCreation;
    thread.thread_creation.process_id = pid;
    thread.thread_creation.thread_id = tid;
    QueryPerformanceFrequency(&thread.thread_creation.creation_time);
    if ( ! WriteData(thread) ) {
      std::println(stderr, "WriteFile() failed with error {}", GetLastError());
    }
    Sleep(1000);


    Message image_load{};
    //this was poor naming...
    image_load.tag = Tag::ImageLoad;
    image_load.creation.process_id = pid;
    QueryPerformanceFrequency(&image_load.image_load.load_time);
    image_load.image_load.image_load = ImageLoad::Clr;
    if ( ! WriteData(image_load) ) {
      std::println(stderr, "WriteFile() failed with error {}", GetLastError());
    }


    Sleep(3000);
  }

  if ( g_ConnectionPort != nullptr )
    CloseHandle(g_ConnectionPort);
}




```

`Thread.cc`:

```cc
#include <Thread.hh>

/**
 * @brief increments counter for given image_load
 * @param image_load Image load can be Clr, WinHttp, WinInet
 */
void Thread::IncrementCount(const ImageLoad image_load) {
    ++events_count_[image_load];
}

/**
 * Insert Imageload that loaded from this thread.
 * @param image_load Image load can be Clr, WinHttp, WinInet
 */
void Thread::InsertImageLoad(ImageLoad image_load) {
  if (!image_loads_.contains(image_load)) {
    image_loads_.insert(image_load);
  }
}

bool Thread::HasImageLoad(ImageLoad image_load) const{
  return image_loads_.contains(image_load);
}


/**
 * @brief Gets the event count for given image load
 * @param image_load Image load can be Clr, WinHttp, WinInet
 * @return int event count if it exists, 0 if not.
 * @TODO this could be the cause of some FPs when just returning 0;
 */
unsigned int Thread::GetEventCount(const ImageLoad image_load) const  {
  if (const auto it = events_count_.find(image_load); it != events_count_.end()) {
    return it->second;
  }
  return 0;
}

/**
 * @brief Get the creation time for the thread
 * @return returns creation_time_
 */
std::time_t Thread::GetCreationTime() const {
  return creation_time_;
}
```

`Util.cc`:

```cc
#include <Util.hh>

bool GuidCompare(const GUID& guid1, const GUID& guid2) {
  return std::memcmp(&guid1, &guid2, sizeof(GUID)) == 0;
}

std::time_t LargeIntToTimeT(const LARGE_INTEGER time) {
  return (time.QuadPart / 10000000) - 11644473600;
}
```

`lib/krabs/README.md`:

```md
# Krabs Readme

Important Preprocessor Definitions:

* `UNICODE` - krabsetw expects the `UNICODE` preprocessor definition to be
  defined. The code will not successfully compile without this flag. There is
  no plan to support compilation without `UNICODE` being set.

* `NDEBUG` - Set this variable in release builds to disable runtime type
   assertions. You'll still get a runtime error if the size type you're
   requesting is not the same size as the property in the event schema.

* `TYPEASSERT` - Set this variable only in debug builds (not `NDEBUG`) to enable
   strict assertions. This means that if an explicit type check is not defined
   for a requested type, a `static_assert` is thrown and the code will not 
   compile until one is added. This is mainly used for krabs development to
   ensure that we don't miss asserts for types that are supported.

```

`lib/krabs/krabs/collection_view.hpp`:

```hpp
// Copyright (c) Microsoft. All rights reserved.
// Licensed under the MIT license. See LICENSE file in the project root for full license information.

#pragma once

#include <string>

#include "compiler_check.hpp"

namespace krabs {

    /**
     * Wraps a range of a collection starting at the location
     * specified by the begin iterator and ending a the location
     * specified by the end iterator. The underlying items are
     * left in-place and should be considered const
     */
    template <typename T>
    struct collection_view
    {
    private:
        const T beg_;
        const T end_;

    public:
        /**
         * Construct a new view for the range specified by the
         * iterators 'begin' and 'end'
         */
        collection_view(const T begin, const T end)
            : beg_(begin)
            , end_(end)
        { }

        /**
         * Get the iterator for the beginning of the view range
         */
        const T begin() const
        {
            return beg_;
        }

        /**
         * Get the iterator for the end of the view range
         */
        const T end() const
        {
            return end_;
        }
    };

    /**
     * Create a view over the range specified by iterators 'begin' and 'end'
     */
    template <typename T>
    inline collection_view<T> view(const T& begin, const T& end)
    {
        return{ begin, end };
    }

    /**
     * Create a const_iterator view over the specified string
     */
    template <typename T>
    inline collection_view<typename std::basic_string<T>::const_iterator> view(const std::basic_string<T>& string)
    {
        return{ string.cbegin(), string.cend() };
    }

    /**
     * Create a const view over the range starting at 'begin' extending 'length' items
     */
    template <typename T>
    inline collection_view<const T*> view(const T* begin, size_t length)
    {
        return{ begin, begin + length };
    }

    /**
     * Create a const view over the specified array
     */
    template <typename T, size_t n>
    inline collection_view<const T*> view(const T(&arr)[n])
    {
        return{ arr, arr + n };
    }

} /* namespace krabs */
```
